[Roy Belson]: It has been my privilege and honor

[Roy Belson]: to be an educator in Medford, in the Medford Public Schools, for 50 years, and to serve as superintendent of schools, your superintendent of schools, for 23 years.

[Roy Belson]: I've greatly benefited from the high quality and diligence of professionals, support staff, school committee members, and citizens who have worked with me throughout my career.

[Roy Belson]: And I am internally grateful to them for making my tenure and responsibilities

[Roy Belson]: as productive and as rewarding as reasonably possible.

[Roy Belson]: I've been very fortunate to have seen former students become teachers, administrators, and staff in our schools.

[Roy Belson]: I've had the experience of enrolling children and grandchildren of former students.

[Roy Belson]: While no one does significant work alone, I've had the opportunity to build new schools, establish a full range of programs, acquire hundreds of millions of dollars in grants,

[Roy Belson]: for our community and school district.

[Roy Belson]: Understandably, there's room for improvement, but much has been done and more will be done in the months ahead.

[Roy Belson]: No one gets to finish everything, but we have put a lot in place and that will be a solid foundation for the future.

[Roy Belson]: Therefore, I am here informing the Medford School Committee

[Roy Belson]: that it's my intention to retire from the position of superintendent of schools, Medford Public Schools, at the completion of my contract on June 30th, 2018.

[Roy Belson]: This decision has been made without reference to any governmental change or any issues that are in our community.

[Roy Belson]: It is simply the right period of time for me to spend more time with my family and to pursue special causes and interests

[Roy Belson]: that have not been possible given the schedule and work responsibilities of an active school superintendent.

[Roy Belson]: It is my intent and plan to be fully engaged in the months ahead as your superintendent.

[Roy Belson]: We have a lot of positive opportunities, some of which we've talked about tonight, ahead of us.

[Roy Belson]: And I will do everything possible to optimize and achieve our goals.

[Roy Belson]: Furthermore, I will be committed to ensuring a smooth and effective transition to new senior leadership.
